\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{ * Radix-\/4 FFT algorithm used is :}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{ * Input real and imaginary data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n) = xa + j * ya}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+N/4 ) = xb + j * yb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+N/2 ) = xc + j * yc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+3N 4) = xd + j * yd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{ * Output real and imaginary data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r) = xa'+ j * ya'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+1) = xb'+ j * yb'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+2) = xc'+ j * yc'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+3) = xd'+ j * yd'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{ * Twiddle factors for radix-\/4 FFT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{ * Wn = co1 + j * (-\/ si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{ * W2n = co2 + j * (-\/ si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{ * W3n = co3 + j * (-\/ si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{ * The real and imaginary output values for the radix-\/4 butterfly are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{ * xa' = xa + xb + xc + xd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{ * ya' = ya + yb + yc + yd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{ * xb' = (xa+yb-\/xc-\/yd)* co1 + (ya-\/xb-\/yc+xd)* (si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{ * yb' = (ya-\/xb-\/yc+xd)* co1 -\/ (xa+yb-\/xc-\/yd)* (si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{ * xc' = (xa-\/xb+xc-\/xd)* co2 + (ya-\/yb+yc-\/yd)* (si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{ * yc' = (ya-\/yb+yc-\/yd)* co2 -\/ (xa-\/xb+xc-\/xd)* (si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{ * xd' = (xa-\/yb-\/xc+yd)* co3 + (ya+xb-\/yc-\/xd)* (si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{ * yd' = (ya+xb-\/yc-\/xd)* co3 -\/ (xa-\/yb-\/xc+yd)* (si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00137}00137 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00977}00977 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00978}00978 \textcolor{comment}{ * Radix-\/4 IFFT algorithm used is :}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00979}00979 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00980}00980 \textcolor{comment}{ * CIFFT uses same twiddle coefficients as CFFT function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00981}00981 \textcolor{comment}{ *  x[k] = x[n] + (j)k * x[n + fftLen/4] + (-\/1)k * x[n+fftLen/2] + (-\/j)k * x[n+3*fftLen/4]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00982}00982 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00983}00983 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00984}00984 \textcolor{comment}{ * IFFT is implemented with following changes in equations from FFT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00985}00985 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00986}00986 \textcolor{comment}{ * Input real and imaginary data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00987}00987 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n) = xa + j * ya}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00988}00988 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+N/4 ) = xb + j * yb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00989}00989 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+N/2 ) = xc + j * yc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00990}00990 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(n+3N 4) = xd + j * yd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00991}00991 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00992}00992 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00993}00993 \textcolor{comment}{ * Output real and imaginary data:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00994}00994 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r) = xa'+ j * ya'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00995}00995 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+1) = xb'+ j * yb'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00996}00996 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+2) = xc'+ j * yc'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00997}00997 \textcolor{comment}{ * x(4r+3) = xd'+ j * yd'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00998}00998 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l00999}00999 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01000}01000 \textcolor{comment}{ * Twiddle factors for radix-\/4 IFFT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01001}01001 \textcolor{comment}{ * Wn = co1 + j * (si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01002}01002 \textcolor{comment}{ * W2n = co2 + j * (si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01003}01003 \textcolor{comment}{ * W3n = co3 + j * (si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01004}01004 \textcolor{comment}{ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01005}01005 \textcolor{comment}{ * The real and imaginary output values for the radix-\/4 butterfly are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01006}01006 \textcolor{comment}{ * xa' = xa + xb + xc + xd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01007}01007 \textcolor{comment}{ * ya' = ya + yb + yc + yd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01008}01008 \textcolor{comment}{ * xb' = (xa-\/yb-\/xc+yd)* co1 -\/ (ya+xb-\/yc-\/xd)* (si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01009}01009 \textcolor{comment}{ * yb' = (ya+xb-\/yc-\/xd)* co1 + (xa-\/yb-\/xc+yd)* (si1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01010}01010 \textcolor{comment}{ * xc' = (xa-\/xb+xc-\/xd)* co2 -\/ (ya-\/yb+yc-\/yd)* (si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01011}01011 \textcolor{comment}{ * yc' = (ya-\/yb+yc-\/yd)* co2 + (xa-\/xb+xc-\/xd)* (si2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01012}01012 \textcolor{comment}{ * xd' = (xa+yb-\/xc-\/yd)* co3 -\/ (ya-\/xb-\/yc+xd)* (si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01013}01013 \textcolor{comment}{ * yd' = (ya-\/xb-\/yc+xd)* co3 + (xa+yb-\/xc-\/yd)* (si3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01014}01014 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__cfft__radix4__q15_8c_source_l01015}01015 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
